      <p><b>Abkhazia</b><sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">[a]</a></sup> (<span class="rt-commentedText nowrap"><span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">/<span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="/æ/: 'a' in 'bad'">æ</span><span title="'b' in 'buy'">b</span><span title="/ˈ/: primary stress follows">ˈ</span><span title="'k' in 'kind'">k</span><span title="/ɑː/: 'a' in 'father'">ɑː</span><span title="'z' in 'zoom'">z</span><span title="/i/: 'y' in 'happy'">i</span><span title="/ə/: 'a' in 'about'">ə</span></span>/</a></span> <span class="nowrap" style="font-size:85%">(<span class="unicode haudio"><span class="fn"><span style="white-space:nowrap;margin-right:.25em;"><a href="/wiki/File:En-Abkhazia-pronunciation.ogg" title="About this sound"><img alt="About this sound" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/11px-Loudspeaker.svg.png" decoding="async" width="11" height="11" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/17px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/22px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="20" data-file-height="20"></a></span><a href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/bd/En-Abkhazia-pronunciation.ogg" class="internal" title="En-Abkhazia-pronunciation.ogg">listen</a></span></span>)</span></span><sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">[10]</a></sup> or <span class="rt-commentedText nowrap"><span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">/<span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="/æ/: 'a' in 'bad'">æ</span><span title="'b' in 'buy'">b</span><span title="/ˈ/: primary stress follows">ˈ</span><span title="'k' in 'kind'">k</span><span title="/eɪ/: 'a' in 'face'">eɪ</span><span title="'z' in 'zoom'">z</span><span title="/i/: 'y' in 'happy'">i</span><span title="/ə/: 'a' in 'about'">ə</span></span>/</a></span></span><sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">[11]</a></sup>) is a <a href="/wiki/De_facto" title="De facto">partially recognized</a> state in the <a href="/wiki/South_Caucasus" class="mw-redirect" title="South Caucasus">South Caucasus</a>, <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Abkhazia_and_South_Ossetia" title="International recognition of Abkhazia and South Ossetia">recognised</a> by most countries as part of <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a>, which views the region as an <a href="/wiki/Government_of_the_Autonomous_Republic_of_Abkhazia" title="Government of the Autonomous Republic of Abkhazia">autonomous republic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Constitution_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Constitution-13">[12]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Faultlines_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Faultlines-14">[13]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Clogg_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Clogg-15">[14]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Karagiannis_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Karagiannis-16">[15]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Olympics_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Olympics-17">[16]</a></sup> It lies on the eastern coast of the <a href="/wiki/Black_Sea" title="Black Sea">Black Sea</a>, south of the <a href="/wiki/Greater_Caucasus" title="Greater Caucasus">Greater Caucasus</a> mountains in northwestern <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a>. It covers 8,665 square kilometres (3,346&nbsp;sq&nbsp;mi) and has a population of around 245,000. Its capital is <a href="/wiki/Sukhumi" title="Sukhumi">Sukhumi</a>. </p>
      <p>The status of Abkhazia is a central issue of the <a href="/wiki/Georgian%E2%80%93Abkhazian_conflict" class="mw-redirect" title="Georgian–Abkhazian conflict">Georgian–Abkhazian conflict</a> and <a href="/wiki/Georgia%E2%80%93Russia_relations" title="Georgia–Russia relations">Georgia–Russia relations</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Polity" title="Polity">polity</a> is <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Abkhazia_and_South_Ossetia" title="International recognition of Abkhazia and South Ossetia">recognised as a state</a> by Russia, Venezuela, Nicaragua, Nauru and Syria. While Georgia lacks control over Abkhazia, the <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Georgia_(country)" title="Government of Georgia (country)">Georgian government</a> and most <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> member states consider Abkhazia legally part of Georgia, with Georgia maintaining an official <a href="/wiki/Government_of_the_Autonomous_Republic_of_Abkhazia" title="Government of the Autonomous Republic of Abkhazia">government-in-exile</a>. </p>
      <p>The region <a href="/wiki/Abkhaz_Autonomous_Soviet_Socialist_Republic" title="Abkhaz Autonomous Soviet Socialist Republic">had autonomy</a> within <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Georgia" class="mw-redirect" title="Soviet Georgia">Soviet Georgia</a> at the time when the <a href="/wiki/Dissolution_of_the_Soviet_Union" title="Dissolution of the Soviet Union">Soviet Union began to disintegrate</a> in the late 1980s. Simmering ethnic tensions between the <a href="/wiki/Abkhazians" title="Abkhazians">Abkhaz</a>—the region's <a href="/wiki/Titular_ethnicity" class="mw-redirect" title="Titular ethnicity">titular ethnicity</a>—and <a href="/wiki/Georgian_people" class="mw-redirect" title="Georgian people">Georgians</a>—the largest single ethnic group at that time—culminated in the <a href="/wiki/1992%E2%80%931993_War_in_Abkhazia" class="mw-redirect" title="1992–1993 War in Abkhazia">1992–1993 War in Abkhazia</a>, which resulted in Georgia's loss of control over most of Abkhazia and the <a href="/wiki/Ethnic_cleansing_of_Georgians_in_Abkhazia" title="Ethnic cleansing of Georgians in Abkhazia">ethnic cleansing of Georgians from Abkhazia</a>. </p>
      <p>Despite a <a href="/wiki/Agreement_on_a_Cease-fire_and_Separation_of_Forces" title="Agreement on a Cease-fire and Separation of Forces">1994 ceasefire agreement</a> and years of negotiations, the dispute remains unresolved. The long-term presence of <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Observer_Mission_in_Georgia" title="United Nations Observer Mission in Georgia">a United Nations Observer Mission</a> and a Russian-led <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Independent_States" title="Commonwealth of Independent States">Commonwealth of Independent States</a> (CIS) peacekeeping force failed to prevent the flare-up of violence on several occasions. In August 2008, Abkhaz and Russian forces fought <a href="/wiki/Russo-Georgian_War" title="Russo-Georgian War">a war</a> against Georgian forces, which led to the formal recognition of Abkhazia by Russia, the annulment of the 1994 ceasefire agreement and the termination of the UN mission. On 28 August 2008, the <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Georgia" title="Parliament of Georgia">Parliament of Georgia</a> declared Abkhazia a <a href="/wiki/Occupied_territories_of_Georgia" title="Occupied territories of Georgia">Russian-occupied territory</a>, a position reflected by most United Nations member states.<sup id="cite_ref-golos-ameriki_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-golos-ameriki-18">[17]</a></sup> </p> 
      <div id="toc" class="toc" role="navigation" aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading">
